// JOB SYSGEN8B   $$BDITFP  DITTO FILE PROTECT TRANSIENT                12.03.09

                                      2 *********************************************************************** $$FP0006
                                      3 *                                                                     * $$FP0007
                                      4 *        THIS  B-TRANSIENT IS FETCHED BY THE PROBLEM PROGRAM 'DITTO', * $$FP0008
                                      5 *        TO LOAD DISK FILE EXTENTS WHEN OPERATING IN A FILE PROTECTED * $$FP0009
                                      6 *        ENVIRONMENT. THESE EXTENTS WILL BE DEQUED BY JOB CONTROL     * $$FP0010
                                      7 *        AT EOJ TIME.                                                 * $$FP0011
                                      8 *        INFORMATION PASSED TO THE TRANSIENT:                         * $$FP0012
                                      9 *             REG  0  POINTS TO AN 8 BYTE PASS FIELD:                 * $$FP0013
                                     10 *                  FIELD BYTE 0-3 = ADDRESS OF THE DESIRED LUB        * $$FP0014
                                     11 *                  FIELD BYTE 4-7 = FILE MASK  (LIMITS AND            * $$FP0015
                                     12 *                   PARTITION OWNERSHIP CODE).                        * $$FP0016
                                     13 *        INFORMATION RETURNED TO DITTO:                               * $$FP0017
                                     14 *             HEX FF RETURN TO BYTE 0 OF THE FILE MASK IF NO          * $$FP0018
                                     15 *                   JIBS ARE AVAILABLE.                               * $$FP0019
                                     16 *        PROCEDURE:                                                   * $$FP0020
                                     17 *             1. CHECK LUB FOR AN ATTACHED JIB.                       * $$FP0021
                                     18 *             2. IF NONE, OBTAIN AND ATTACH JIB AND LOAD XTENTS IN JIB* $$FP0022
                                     19 *             3. IF JIB IS ATTACHED, FOLLOW JIB CHAIN UNTIL XTENT TYPE* $$FP0023
                                     20 *                LOCATED OR END OF CHAIN REACHED.                     * $$FP0024
                                     21 *             4. IF XTENT TYPE, INCREASE LIMITS TO MAXIMUM.           * $$FP0025
                                     22 *             5. IF END OF CHAIN, ATTACH JIB AND LOAD XTENTS.         * $$FP0026
                                     23 *                                                                     * $$FP0027
                                     24 *              C. A. ALEXANDER     IBM     DETROIT, MICHIGAN          * $$FP0028
                                     25 *********************************************************************** $$FP0029
